\operatorname{dn}\left( {u + v}\right)  = \frac{\left( {\operatorname{dn}u}\right) \left( {\operatorname{dn}v}\right)  - {k}^{2}\left( {\operatorname{sn}u}\right) \left( {\operatorname{cn}u}\right) \left( {\operatorname{sn}v}\right) \left( {\operatorname{cn}v}\right) }{1 - {k}^{2}\left( {{\operatorname{sn}}^{2}u}\right) \left( {{\operatorname{sn}}^{2}v}\right) }, \tag{14.111c}
$$

(3) ${\left( \operatorname{sn}z\right) }^{\prime } = \left( {\operatorname{cn}z}\right) \left( {\operatorname{dn}z}\right)$ ,(14.112a)

$$
{\left( \operatorname{cn}z\right) }^{\prime } =  - \left( {\operatorname{sn}z}\right) \left( {\operatorname{dn}z}\right) , \tag{14.112b}
$$

$$
{\left( \operatorname{dn}z\right) }^{\prime } =  - {k}^{2}\left( {\operatorname{sn}z}\right) \left( {\operatorname{cn}z}\right) . \tag{14.112c}
$$

雅可比函数的其他性质和另一些椭圆函数见 [14.10], [14.18].

![0193686a-f46c-7301-ad92-9f1def8f454e_183_612_915_419_256_0.jpg](images/0193686a-f46c-7301-ad92-9f1def8f454e_183_612_915_419_256_0.jpg)

图 14.56

#### 14.6.3 $\theta$ 函数

可以用 $\theta$ 函数 (theta functions) 来计算雅可比函数:

$$
{\vartheta }_{1}\left( {z, q}\right)  = 2{q}^{\frac{1}{4}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{\left( -1\right) }^{n}{q}^{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }\sin \left( {{2n} + 1}\right) z, \tag{14.113a}
$$

$$
{\vartheta }_{2}\left( {z, q}\right)  = 2{q}^{\frac{1}{4}}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 0}}^{\infty }{q}^{n\left( {n + 1}\right) }\cos \left( {{2n} + 1}\right) z, \tag{14.113b}
$$

$$
{\vartheta }_{3}\left( {z, q}\right)  = 1 + 2\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 1}}^{\infty }{q}^{{n}^{2}}\cos {2nz}, \tag{14.113c}
$$

$$
{\vartheta }_{4}\left( {z, q}\right)  = 1 + 2\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{n = 1}}^{\infty }{\left( -1\right) }^{n}{q}^{{n}^{2}}\cos {2nz}. \tag{14.113d}
$$

如果 $\left| q\right|  < 1$ ( $q$ 是复数),则级数 $\left( {{14.113}\mathrm{a}}\right)  \sim  \left( {{14.113}\mathrm{\;d}}\right)$ 对于每个复变量 $z$ 都是收敛的. 当 $q$ 是常数的情形,用下述简单的记号:

$$
{\vartheta }_{k}\left( z\right)  \mathrel{\text{:=}} {\vartheta }_{k}\left( {{\pi z}, q}\right) \;\left( {k = 1,2,3,4}\right) . \tag{14.114}
$$

此时, 雅可比函数有表达式:

$$
\operatorname{sn}z = {2K}\frac{{\vartheta }_{4}\left( 0\right) }{{\vartheta }_{1}^{\prime }\left( 0\right) }\frac{{\vartheta }_{1}\left( \frac{z}{2K}\right) }{{\vartheta }_{4}\left( \frac{z}{2K}\right) }, \tag{14.115a}
$$

$$
\operatorname{cn}z = \frac{{\vartheta }_{4}\left( 0\right) }{{\vartheta }_{2}\left( 0\right) }\frac{{\vartheta }_{2}\left( \frac{z}{2K}\right) }{{\vartheta }_{4}\left( \frac{z}{2K}\right) }, \tag{14.115b}
$$

$$
\operatorname{dn}z = \frac{{\vartheta }_{4}\left( 0\right) }{{\vartheta }_{3}\left( 0\right) }\frac{{\vartheta }_{3}\left( \frac{z}{2K}\right) }{{\vartheta }_{4}\left( \frac{z}{2K}\right) }, \tag{14.115c}
$$

其中

$$
q = \exp \left( {-\pi \frac{{K}^{\prime }}{K}}\right) ,\;k = {\left( \frac{{\vartheta }_{2}\left( 0\right) }{{\vartheta }_{3}\left( 0\right) }\right) }^{2}, \tag{14.115d}
$$

以及 $K,{K}^{\prime }$ 如 (14.109) 所述.

#### 14.6.4 魏尔斯特拉斯函数

魏尔斯特拉斯引进了函数

$$
\wp \left( z\right)  = \wp \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right) , \tag{14.116a}
$$

$$
\zeta \left( z\right)  = \zeta \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right) , \tag{14.116b}
$$

$$
\sigma \left( z\right)  = \sigma \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right) , \tag{14.116c}
$$

这里 ${\omega }_{1}$ 和 ${\omega }_{2}$ 是其商非实数的两个任意复数. 做代换

$$
{\omega }_{mn} = 2\left( {m{\omega }_{1} + n{\omega }_{2}}\right) , \tag{14.117a}
$$

其中 $m$ 和 $n$ 是任意整数,并定义

$$
\wp \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right)  = {z}^{-2} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m, n}}{}^{\prime }\left\lbrack  {{\left( z - {\omega }_{mn}\right) }^{-2} - {\omega }_{mn}^{-2}}\right\rbrack  . \tag{14.117b}
$$

求和号后面的撇表示忽略 $m = n = 0$ 项. 函数 $\wp \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right)$ 有下列性质:

(1) 它是一个有周期 ${\omega }_{1}$ 和 ${\omega }_{2}$ 的椭圆函数.

(2) 对于每个 $z \neq  {\omega }_{mn}$ ,级数 (14.117b) 收敛.

(3) 函数 $\wp \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right)$ 满足微分方程

$$
{\wp }^{\prime 2} = 4{\wp }^{3} - {g}_{2}\wp  - {g}_{3}, \tag{14.118a}
$$

其中

$$
{g}_{2} = {60}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m, n}}{}^{\prime }{\omega }_{mn}^{-4},\;{g}_{3} = {140}\mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m, n}}{}^{\prime }{\omega }_{mn}^{-6}. \tag{14.118b}
$$

量 ${g}_{2}$ 和 ${g}_{3}$ 被称为 $\wp \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right)$ 的不变量 (invariants).

(4) 函数 $\wp \left( {z,{\omega }_{1},{\omega }_{2}}\right)$ 是积分

$$
z = {\int }_{u}^{\infty }\frac{\mathrm{d}t}{\sqrt{4{t}^{3} - {g}_{2}t - {g}_{3}}} \tag{14.119}
$$

的反函数.

$$
\text{(5)}\wp \left( {u + v}\right)  = \frac{1}{4}{\left\lbrack  \frac{{\wp }^{\prime }\left( u\right)  - {\wp }^{\prime }\left( v\right) }{\wp \left( u\right)  - \wp \left( v\right) }\right\rbrack  }^{2} - \wp \left( u\right)  - \wp \left( v\right) \text{.} \tag{14.120}
$$

魏尔斯特拉斯函数

$$
\zeta \left( z\right)  = {z}^{-1} + \mathop{\sum }\limits_{{m, n}}{}^{\prime }\left\lbrack  {{\left( z - {\omega }_{mn}\right) }^{-1} + {\omega }_{mn}^{-1} + {\omega }_{mn}^{-2}z}\right\rbrack  , \tag{14.121a}
$$

$$
\sigma \left( z\right)  = z\exp \left( {{\int }_{0}^{z}\left\lbrack  {\zeta \left( t\right)  - {t}^{-1}}\right\rbrack  \mathrm{d}t}\right)
$$

$$
= z\mathop{\prod }\limits_{{m, n}}{}^{\prime }\left( {1 - \frac{z}{{\omega }_{mn}}}\right) \exp \left( {\frac{z}{{\omega }_{mn}} + \frac{{z}^{2}}{2{\omega }_{mn}^{2}}}\right)  \tag{14.121b}
$$

不是双周期的, 因而它们不是椭圆函数. 下列关系式成立:

(1) ${\zeta }^{\prime }\left( z\right)  =  - \wp \left( z\right) ,\;\zeta \left( z\right)  = \ln \sigma \left( z\right)$ ;(14.122)

(2) $\zeta \left( {-z}\right)  =  - \zeta \left( z\right) ,\;\sigma \left( {-z}\right)  =  - \sigma \left( z\right)$ ;(14.123)

(3) $\zeta \left( {z + 2{\omega }_{1}}\right)  = \zeta \left( z\right)  + {2\zeta }\left( {\omega }_{1}\right) ,\;\zeta \left( {z + 2{\omega }_{2}}\right)  = \zeta \left( z\right)  + {2\zeta }\left( {\omega }_{2}\right)$ ;(14.124)

(4) $\zeta \left( {u + v}\right)  = \zeta \left( u\right)  + \zeta \left( v\right)  + \frac{1}{2}\frac{{\wp }^{\prime }\left( u\right)  - {\wp }^{\prime }\left( v\right) }{\wp \left( u\right)  - \wp \left( v\right) }$ ;(14.125)

(5) 每个椭圆函数是魏尔斯特拉斯函数 $\wp \left( z\right)$ 和 $\zeta \left( z\right)$ 的有理函数.
